< review>
Fro & the whole staff are great!. Fun to interact with them. Love that they incorporate the fruits and veggies that grow there into the menu. Had so many tasty dishes there. Some of the best local beer insider selections. I don't even like cider and the ones he carries I crave. He smokes his own meats too! It's a little paradise getaway in West Sac.

It's such a charming place with the trees being 90 years old!

I've never been a regular anywhere I have lived but it's time I am and I choose here.

I would suggest the two tables in the center near the vegetable garden should have umbrellas at tilt to block the midday sun. You can see them in the first 2 photos. The back left corner table is MINE! üòÅ<//review>

My root-canaled tooth is intact.  The endodontist just drilled a tiny hole in the back.

Then, Dr. Fung did bleach treatments INSIDE my dead tooth, to keep it from being discolored.  No, my teeth are not all pearly white.  My tooth looks just like it did before the root canal.  That's what I needed.  That's what I can afford.

I found Dr. Fung on instagram.  When I was searching for help with my root canal...his page popped up in my feed. <Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
"Dr. Ray" as he goes by for the kids is a father of two. He's the real deal and amazing at what he does. His own father was a dentist, so he has answered a family calling which suits him naturally. Along with his training at one of the country's top dental schools, he has the perfect touch and tone with children. He never talks down to your child, but speaks directly to them as an equal with a natural manner that puts them at ease. He lets a child warm up to him at their own speed.

We were referred to Dr. Klein after a negative experience at another office. The previous doctor and staff missed a major cavity molar that we spotted the weekend right after her annual check up. On top of that, when my wife took her back, the doctor told us he would have to do a root canal, lectured her and was even short with my daughter for taking one too many stickers. So we were all in a vulnerable place.

What a breath of fresh air Dr. Klein was in contrast. First, he told us he would not automatically do a root canal but would examine things closer up. Upon further examination of her X-rays and when we came in, he determined a root canal was overkill. He took the time to answer all of my wife's questions without being condescending, but with actual interest and curiosity. She was also able to sit with my daughter during the fillings, as he explained each step of the process to her. He's a wizard at administering the initial Novocain shot, which she was certain would scare my daughter. She didn't even notice it. She did not flinch or cry. She says he truly has a masterful hand and would not have believed it if she had not seen it.

She was expecting the the fillings procedure to be at the very least slightly traumatic for our four-year-old, but instead it was a pleasant and positive experience, where we were given great advice and support before, during and after. Our daughter's view of her new dentist, Dr. Klein is fun loving and trusting. She calls him fondly "Dr. Ray."

The office staff is also great, helpful, patient, and genuinely cheerful. The office space is modern with a waiting room that is quirky cool and stocked with (clean!) and clever toys your kids will actually want to play with. The entire appointment was scheduled to take one hour and it did on the nose, even with all the questions and allowing time for my daughter to settle in. Time by went by without anxiety. We were never rushed.

Leaving this office, you realize everyone is there because they truly enjoy and take pride in their work. And they should because there is tremendous value in what they do. Thank you, Dr. Ray and team!< /Text>

<review>Continuing my fried chicken sandwich tour, I came to Kluckin Chicken after choosing it from the plethora of options available in LA. <username>Mike Ziolek<//username><time>1593630007473<//time><response>None<//response><Review>Unique "street food/outdoor restaurant" that is a car wash by day and converts over in the evening to serve up tasty hot chicken. Easy to get to right off of exit 16 going south on 101 (you'll see them cooking up their culinary goodness from the exit ramp). Having had fried chicken from Boston to Los Angeles and everywhere in-between, I can definitely say Hot Motha Clucker is high up on my list for a particular flavor.

For a first time, I'd suggest trying the two tender meal. It'll let you get a taste of their chicken (this is boneless tender chicken) on buttered toast. Make sure you make it a doozy (adds cheese and honey for an extra two bucks). Another option to try is the saucy, never dry Chef Special. You'll get a unique combination of their tasty fried chicken chopped and mixed into a grilled cheese, all nestled between two slices of buttery toast. Both of these come by default with their crispy and salty fries.

Oh, and when the person handing out your order asks if you want sauces, make sure you say yes. Nothing like being able to dip a salty french fry or fried pickle into soothing cool ranch sauce or their peppery ranch variety (they'll give you both by default).< /Review><gmap_id>0x80c297b9f032979b:0x5b9199a4315122d8<//gmap_id><Rating>5</Rating></record></dataset><record>

< Text>
If you are looking for a super delicious fried chicken sandwich that's seasoned to perfection, then Hot Motha Clucker is your kind of place. Located outside of a carwash, this place not only delivers mouthwatering chicken in various spiciness levels and seasonings but also provides very friendly customer service. I've tried almost everything on their menu, but the original chef special is my favorite. I highly recommend them especially for late-night munchies as they're open late.</Text>

<userid>113669553636359461479<//userid><user_name>Steve Cha</user_name><Date>1564203420378<//Date><rating>5< /rating>< Review>
Awesome chicken. Been here 3 times already and still can't get enough of it. I tried the slider combo and the tender combo. I would recommend the tender combo more because it seems like a better deal. The tenders have a great taste and crisp to it, along with some nice fries and pickles. The only thing is be prepared to wait, as it can be up to 30 minutes sometimes, since they cook everything from scratch. I shot a YouTube video on my channel Rockstar Eater if you want to see an overview of the facility and food!</Review>

<Review>The energy at this F45 studio is contagious - and that's ALWAYS a good thing!! I've been coming to the Hillcrest location for over a year & I'm also one of the DJs for Saturday classes - the vibe that this place has is second to none (from the owners to the members). I've been to several other F45 studios in SD, and the trainers here are just on a different level; whereas other places may tell you to go "faster faster!" to get as many reps in & get your heart rate up, here the focus is on quality, not quantity - they help the clients, no matter their level of fitness, maintain good form throughout the set and suggest any modifications as needed. This is really important, especially in a group setting. The workouts are always intense - I've been doing F45 since June 2017, and they never get easier. It's good to see the trainers always challenge even the more advanced members. They are also very passionate about the program, and that's evident from the enthusiasm they bring to the classes. The studio also hosts various social events throughout the year such as beach workouts and comedy nights which help to keep the feel of a strong community.

Nowadays with COVID, the studio has done a phenomenal job with making the necessary modifications to maintain social distancing and cleanliness (it has always been clean!). We are all spaced at least 6 feet apart and have all the equipment we need in our tile, so no rotating/sharing equipment which was the case pre-COVID. Cleaning solution is also at each tile, and we all clean our equipment thoroughly at the end of the class. The trainers will then do another cleaning immediately after and before the next class. I have zero hesitation coming here during these current times.

Yes, I'd highly recommend this studio to anyone looking for a group training setting. I could have asked to DJ at several other F45 studios in SD, but from their social media content I knew the Hillcrest location was a step above the rest. I believe the studio is the largest F45 in the city - another perk to consider!

**Note - the DJ pics are pre-COVID - as mentioned above, everyone works out in their own square tile now.<//Review><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOZnt06y1FZKVR4yKMM6Rn9pOnzSqOREm-AuoIQ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPG7YQw2T8gm4vCJeIayNuzkSB07BRW0uKOY6vx=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOcCok_Pp36hfvPSkgDXt98ofQ2Ksu0YdbEMyns=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</Pictures>< Response>

Love this place!

I come here pretty regularly. Almost every Monday and whenever I have extra time to do some work or maybe just pick up a coffee.

They're Guatemalan and the other one I unfortunately cannot remember was really good.

Lattes are good. Not much caffeine if that's what your looking for. The Gibraltar had a strong taste but seemed to do there caffeine job for a a bit longer.

<Time>1441003727690<//Time><rate>5</rate><Review>Sometimes you only have to go a place once to know how great it is and Easy Bay Coffee Co meets those exceptions. Located on a quiet corner in Pinole, East Bay Coffee is more than a coffee shop but also a place which holds weekly events: Open Mic on Thursday, Board Game Wednesdays, and Worship on Sundays.

There is not a lot of parking provided from the shop, however there is plenty of parking nearby and across the street. As I walked into the place you immediately get a relax and friendly vibe. There is plenty of seating and limited outlets. It's a great place to study or have a quiet chat with a friend.

As for the coffee (I.E. vanilla latte) it was refreshing and packed with caffeine because I was wired the rest of the night and the cheesecake was mind-blowing delicious; the price for all of this was $10. The pricing is a little high, I think it's worth it. The service is also great, very friendly. I understand why this place gets so many visitors and is beloved by the locals. East Bay Coffee Co is your go-to alternative coffee shop when you want to experience coffee in a home-like atmosphere.<//Review>< Pics>

<Rate>4<//Rate>< Text>
Free WiFi, two bathrooms, tasty pastries, some good coffees, and fun seasonal coffees.

They use single origin coffees, but there's not much variety. Choice of two cold pressed iced coffees, a dark (Sumatra) roast or a blend (East Bay). The hot coffee comes in either a dark (Sumatra) or medium (Guatamala) roast. No fresh made iced coffee with light roast available. No cold brew.

For my tastes they don't seem to offer coffee I love: single origin light roast in either iced or cold brew. BUT, they offer pour over Ethiopian coffee on weekends, which is up my alley.<//Text>

< rate>
5<//rate>
< Text>
We have been coming here since EBCC opened. My daughter recognizes all the awesome staff, since she's basically seen them her whole life. The ambience of EBCC is perfect for fostering a child's ability to order and pay for an order: quiet attention, small town feel, wonderfully caring baristas, with excellent attention to details (like the teddy bear foam picture on the kids hot chocolate).

But it's also amazing for adults! Fresh, delicious, caffeinated beverages. Scrumptious pasteries line the case, including a wonderful chocolate mousse that absolutely hits the spot when I've had a long day with a strong willed child.

They have open mic night, a worship service, and a ukulele play along based lesson. There is so much good stuff going on at EBCC. I hope they are here for many years.<//Text>

< review>
East Bay Coffee House or East Bay Coffee Company is a new edition to Pinole, California.  Pinole, a charming; valley community is the East Bay's best kept secret.

East Bay Coffee House offers its customers a very spacious area (for California) to enjoy their coffees and focus on studying, work, reading,etc.

East Bay Coffee offers Open Mic on Thursdays and for performers who bring their A game to the table, the Coffee House offers an excellent PA / Sound System.  Starbucks and Peets in Pinole are both very small and they do not offer live music.  East Bay Coffee House is Pinole's #1 Coffee Shop!<//review>
